          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.1">athāto dvivraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.3">dvau vraṇau bhavataḥ | śarīrasamutthaś cāgantuś ca tayoḥ
            śarīrasamuttho vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātanimitta āgantukaḥ puruṣa<pc
              > </pc>mṛga<pc> </pc>paśu<pc> </pc>pakṣi<pc> </pc>vyāḍasarīsṛpa<pc

            paraśuśaktikuntādyāyudhaprahareṇābhighātanimittaḥ<lb/> | tatra tulye

            |</l>

            prasṛtasyaupaśamārtham pi<lb/>ttavacchītakriyāvibhāgaḥ | sandhānārthañ ca
            madhughṛtopayoga i<cb/>ti | etad vikāraṇotthānaprayojanam uttarakālan tu
              doṣopaplavaviśeṣā<hi>d avasthāntaraviśeṣāḥ</hi> śārīravat pratīkāraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.5">doṣopaplavaviśeṣaḥ punaḥ samāsa<cb/>taḥ pañcadaśaprakāro
            bhavati | yathokte vraṇapraśnādhyāye prasaraṇasāmarthyāc cha<unclear>ddhaś
              ceti</unclear> ṣoḍaśaprakāra ity ucyate |</l>

            |</l>

            muhu<lb/>rmmuhuḥ śītapicchalāsrāvī ceti vātaśleṣmābhyāṃ || guruḥ
            sa<cb/>dāhoṣṇaḥ pītapāṇḍusrāvī ceti pittaśleṣmābhyāṃ || tanurūkṣastodavahulaḥ
            prasupta iva ca kṛṣṇāru<unclear>ṇā</unclear><lb/> bhastadvvarṇṇasrāvī ceti
            vātaśoṇitābhyāṃ || ghṛtamaṇḍābho mīnadhāvanagandhīmṛdurvvisarppīkṛṣṇoṣṇasrāvī
            ceti pittaśoṇitābhyāṃ || rakto gurusnigdhaḥ kaṇḍūprāyaḥ picchilaḥ sara<pb
              n="200v"/>ktasrāvī ceti śleṣmaśoṇitābhyāṃ | sphuraṇatodadāhadhūmāyanaprāyaḥ

            kaṇḍūsphuraṇacumucumāyamānaprāyaḥ pāṇḍutanuraktasrā<lb/>vī ceti

              nirddarśakanirmmathanasphuraṇatodadāhapā<cb/>karāgakaṇḍū<unclear>vāṃ</unclear>svāpavahulo

            ceti śuddho vraṇaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.1.8">tasyaitasya vraṇasya ṣaṣṭirupakramā bhavanti | tad
            yathā<lb/>patarpaṇamālepanaḥ pariṣeko 'bhyaṅgaḥ svedo vimlāyanam upanā<cb/>ho

          <!-- 229v : 1 -->

          <!--    The vulgate text begins from <xml:id="SS.4.8.4"> but the manuscript has four lines of the text in the  beginning. Hence I have  given new xml ids from SS.4.8.1,  SS.4.8.2, SS.4.8.3 and SS.4.8.3a. Further to this, SS.4.8.23a and SS.4.8.51a are added.

SS.4.8.47cd and SS.4.8.51cd are missing verses.      -->


          <l xml:id="SS.4.8.1"> athāto bhagandarāṇāñ ci-<lb n="2"/>kitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.8.2"> pañca bhagandarā vyākhyātāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.8.3"> teṣv asā<cb/>dhyaḥ śambūkāvarttaḥ śalyanimittaś ca | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.8.3a"> śeṣāḥ kṛcchrasādhyāḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.8.4"> tatra bhagandarapiṭakopadrutam āturam a<lb n="3"
            />patarppaṇād yena virecanāntenaikādaśavidhenopakrameṇopa<cb/>caret |
            apakkvapiṭakaṃ | pakkveṣu copasnigdhamavagāḍhasvinnaṃ śayyāyāṃ
            saṃveśyārśasamiva yantrayi<lb n="4"/>tvā bhagandaram abhis amīkṣya
            parācīnamarvākcīnaṃ bahirmmukha<cb/>mantarmukham vā tataḥ
            prādāyeṣaṇīnnamayitvā śāyasamuddharecchastreṇa | antarmukhañ caivama

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.1"> athāto mūḍhagarbhbhacikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.3"> nātaḥ kaṣṭataramasti yathā mūḍhagarbhbhoddharaṇama<lb
              n="5"/>tra hi yoniyakṛtplīhāntragarbhbhāśayānām madhye kartavyaṃ |
            spa<cb/>rśeno tkarṣāyakarṣaṇāpakarttanabhedanavyāvarttanapīḍanārjjūkaraṇāni
            caikahastena garbhbhamahiṃ<lb n="6"/>satā garbhbhiṇīñ cāhiṃsatā tasmād
              adhikṛtya<add place="below">ta</add>māpṛcchya parañ ca yan
            namāsthāyopakrameta || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.15.4"> tatra samāsenāṣṭavidha mūḍhagarbhbhagatiruddiṣṭā
